##### **From Prototype to Classroom: An Intelligent Tutoring System for Quantum Education**
2604.24807v1 by Iizalaarab Elhaimeur, Nikos Chrisochoides

Quantum computing instructors face a compounding problem: the concepts are counterintuitive, the mathematical formalism is dense, and qualified faculty are scarce outside a small number of well-resourced institutions. Our prior work introduced a knowledge-graph-augmented tutoring prototype with two specialized LLM agents: a Teaching Agent for dynamic interaction and a Lesson Planning Agent for lesson generation. Validated on simulated runs rather than in a real course, that prototype left open whether more aggressive agent specialization would be needed to handle the full range of quantum education tasks under real student load. This paper answers the three questions that the prototype could not answer. Can agent specialization solve the reliability problem in a domain as technically demanding as quantum information science? Can the system run in a real course, not a demonstration? Does the instructor gain actionable intelligence from the deployment? We present ITAS (Intelligent Teaching Assistant System), a multi-agent tutoring system built around four contributions: a five-module QIS curriculum grounded in Watrous's information-first framework, a Spoke-and-Wheel teaching architecture with quantum-specialized agents, a cloud infrastructure designed for production use and regulatory compliance, and a conversational analytics layer for instructors and content developers. Piloted in a quantum computing course at Old Dominion University, the system supports all three answers: deployment evidence is consistent with specialization addressing the task-boundary failures observed in the prototype, cloud infrastructure supports classroom-scale concurrency at sub-textbook cost, and the analytics agent surfaces curriculum gaps the instructor could not otherwise see.

摘要：量子計算的教師面臨一個複雜的問題：這些概念違反直覺，數學形式主義密集，並且合格的教職員在少數資源豐富的機構之外相當稀缺。我們之前的工作介紹了一個知識圖譜增強的輔導原型，該原型有兩個專門的 LLM 代理：一個用於動態互動的教學代理和一個用於課程生成的課程規劃代理。該原型在模擬運行中進行驗證，而不是在真實課程中，這讓人懷疑是否需要更積極的代理專業化來處理在真實學生負載下的全範圍量子教育任務。本文回答了該原型無法回答的三個問題。代理專業化能否解決在量子信息科學這樣技術要求高的領域中的可靠性問題？系統能否在真實課程中運行，而不是演示？教師能否從部署中獲得可行的情報？我們提出了 ITAS（智能教學助手系統），這是一個多代理輔導系統，圍繞四個貢獻構建：基於 Watrous 的信息優先框架的五模塊 QIS 課程，一個具有量子專門代理的輻射式教學架構，設計用於生產使用和合規的雲基礎設施，以及為教師和內容開發者提供的對話分析層。該系統在老道明大學的量子計算課程中進行了試點，支持所有三個答案：部署證據與專業化解決原型中觀察到的任務邊界失敗一致，雲基礎設施支持課堂規模的並發運行，成本低於教科書，並且分析代理揭示了教師無法看到的課程空白。

##### **Factual and Edit-Sensitive Graph-to-Sequence Generation via Graph-Aware Adaptive Noising**
2604.24104v1 by Aditya Hemant Shahane, Anuj Kumar Sirohi, Tanmoy Chakraborty, Prathosh A P, Sandeep Kumar

Fine-tuned autoregressive models for graph-to-sequence generation (G2S) often struggle with factual grounding and edit sensitivity. To tackle these issues, we propose a non-autoregressive diffusion framework that generates text by iterative refinement conditioned on an input graph, named as Diffusion Language Model for Graphs (DLM4G). By aligning graph components (entities/relations) with their corresponding sequence tokens, DLM4G employs an adaptive noising strategy. The proposed strategy uses per-token denoising error as a signal to adaptively modulate noise on entity and relation tokens, improving preservation of graph structure and enabling localized updates under graph edits. Evaluated on three datasets, DLM4G consistently outperforms competitive G2S diffusion baselines trained on identical splits across both surface-form and embedding-based metrics. DLM4G further exceeds fine-tuned autoregressive baselines up to 12x larger (e.g., T5-Large) and is competitive with zero-shot LLM transfer baselines up to 127x larger. Relative to the strongest fine-tuned PLM baseline, DLM4G improves factual grounding (FGT@0.5) by +5.16% and edit sensitivity (ESR) by +7.9%; compared to the best diffusion baseline, it yields gains of +3.75% in FGT@0.5 and +23.6% in ESR. We additionally demonstrate applicability beyond textual graphs through experiments on molecule captioning, indicating the method's generality for scientific G2S generation.

摘要：微調的自回歸模型在圖到序列生成（G2S）中常常面臨事實基礎和編輯敏感性問題。為了解決這些問題，我們提出了一種非自回歸擴散框架，通過基於輸入圖的迭代精煉來生成文本，稱為圖的擴散語言模型（DLM4G）。DLM4G通過將圖元件（實體/關係）與其對應的序列標記對齊，採用了自適應噪聲策略。所提出的策略使用每個標記的去噪誤差作為信號，自適應地調節實體和關係標記上的噪聲，改善圖結構的保留，並在圖編輯下實現局部更新。在三個數據集上的評估中，DLM4G在表面形式和基於嵌入的指標上，始終超越在相同分割上訓練的競爭性G2S擴散基準。DLM4G進一步超越了微調的自回歸基準，後者的規模大達12倍（例如，T5-Large），並且在零樣本LLM轉移基準中與規模達127倍的模型具有競爭力。相對於最強的微調PLM基準，DLM4G在事實基礎（FGT@0.5）上提高了+5.16%，在編輯敏感性（ESR）上提高了+7.9%；與最佳擴散基準相比，它在FGT@0.5上獲得了+3.75%的增益，在ESR上獲得了+23.6%的增益。我們還通過分子標題生成的實驗展示了該方法在文本圖之外的適用性，表明該方法對於科學G2S生成的普遍性。

##### **The Pragmatic Persona: Discovering LLM Persona through Bridging Inference**
2604.24079v1 by Jisoo Yang, Jongwon Ryu, Minuk Ma, Trung X. Pham, Junyeong Kim

Large Language Models (LLMs) reveal inherent and distinctive personas through dialogue. However, most existing persona discovery approaches rely on surface-level lexical or stylistic cues, treating dialogue as a flat sequence of tokens and failing to capture the deeper discourse-level structures that sustain persona consistency. To address this limitation, we propose a novel analytical framework that interprets LLM dialogue through bridging inference -- implicit conceptual relations that connect utterances via shared world knowledge and discourse coherence. By modeling these relations as structured knowledge graphs, our approach captures latent semantic links that govern how LLMs organize meaning across turns, enabling persona discovery at the level of discourse coherence rather than surface realizations. Experimental results across multiple reasoning backbones and target LLMs, ranging from small-scale models to 80B-parameter systems, demonstrate that bridging-inference graphs yield significantly stronger semantic coherence and more stable persona identification than frequency or style-based baselines. These results show that persona traits are consistently encoded in the structural organization of discourse rather than isolated lexical patterns. This work presents a systematic framework for probing, extracting, and visualizing latent LLM personas through the lens of Cognitive Discourse Theory, bridging computational linguistics, cognitive semantics, and persona reasoning in large language models. Codes are available at https://github.com/JiSoo-Yang/Persona_Bridging.git

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）透過對話揭示出固有且獨特的人格特質。<lb/>然而，大多數現有的人格發現方法依賴於表面層的詞彙或風格線索，將對話視為一個平坦的符號序列，未能捕捉到維持人格一致性的更深層對話結構。<lb/>為了解決這一限制，我們提出了一個新穎的分析框架，通過橋接推理來解釋LLM對話——這是通過共享的世界知識和對話連貫性來連接發言的隱含概念關係。<lb/>通過將這些關係建模為結構化知識圖，我們的方法捕捉到潛在的語義聯繫，這些聯繫支配著LLMs如何在輪次之間組織意義，使人格發現能夠在對話連貫性層面進行，而不是表面實現層面。<lb/>在多個推理骨幹和目標LLMs上進行的實驗結果，涵蓋從小型模型到80B參數系統，顯示橋接推理圖在語義連貫性和人格識別的穩定性上顯著優於基於頻率或風格的基準。<lb/>這些結果表明，人格特徵在對話的結構組織中持續編碼，而不是孤立的詞彙模式。<lb/>這項工作提出了一個系統化的框架，通過認知對話理論的視角來探測、提取和可視化潛在的LLM人格，橋接計算語言學、認知語義學和大型語言模型中的人格推理。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/JiSoo-Yang/Persona_Bridging.git 獲得。

##### **Grounding Before Generalizing: How AI Differs from Humans in Causal Transfer**
2604.24062v1 by Liangru Xiang, Yuxi Ma, Zhihao Cao, Yixin Zhu, Song-Chun Zhu

Extracting abstract causal structures and applying them to novel situations is a hallmark of human intelligence. While Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision Language Models (VLMs) have shown strong performance on a wide range of reasoning tasks, their capacity for interactive causal learning -- inducing latent structures through sequential exploration and transferring them across contexts -- remains uncharacterized. Human learners accomplish such transfer after minimal exposure, whereas classical Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents fail catastrophically. Whether state-of-the-art Artificial Intelligence (AI) models possess human-like mechanisms for abstract causal structure transfer is an open question. Using the OpenLock paradigm requiring sequential discovery of Common Cause (CC) and Common Effect (CE) structures, here we show that models exhibit fundamentally delayed or absent transfer: even successful models require initial environmental-specific mapping -- what we term environmental grounding -- before efficiency gains emerge, whereas humans leverage prior structural knowledge from the very first solution attempt. In the text-only condition, models matched or exceeded human discovery efficiency. In contrast, visual information -- in both the image-only and text-and-image conditions -- overall degraded rather than enhanced performance, revealing a broad reliance on symbolic processing rather than integrated multimodal reasoning. Models further exhibited systematic CC/CE asymmetries absent in humans, suggesting heuristic biases rather than direction-neutral causal abstraction. These findings reveal that large-scale statistical learning does not produce the decontextualized causal schemas underpinning human analogical reasoning, establishing grounding-dependent transfer as a fundamental limitation of current LLMs and VLMs.

摘要：提取抽象因果結構並將其應用於新情境是人類智慧的一個特徵。雖然大型語言模型（LLMs）和視覺語言模型（VLMs）在各種推理任務上表現出色，但它們在互動式因果學習方面的能力——通過序列探索誘導潛在結構並在不同上下文中轉移它們——仍然未被表徵。人類學習者在最小的暴露後能夠完成這種轉移，而傳統的強化學習（RL）代理則會遭遇災難性的失敗。最先進的人工智慧（AI）模型是否具有人類類似的抽象因果結構轉移機制仍然是一個未解之謎。使用OpenLock範式，要求對共同原因（CC）和共同效果（CE）結構進行序列發現，我們在此顯示模型表現出根本性延遲或缺失的轉移：即使是成功的模型也需要最初的環境特定映射——我們稱之為環境基礎——才能出現效率增益，而人類則從第一次解決嘗試中利用先前的結構知識。在僅有文本的條件下，模型的發現效率與人類相當或超過。相比之下，視覺信息——在僅有圖像和文本與圖像的條件下——整體上降低了而不是提升了性能，顯示出對符號處理的廣泛依賴，而不是綜合的多模態推理。模型還表現出系統性的CC/CE不對稱，而人類則不存在這種情況，這表明存在啟發式偏見，而不是方向中立的因果抽象。這些發現揭示了大規模統計學習並未產生支撐人類類比推理的去情境化因果模式，確立了依賴基礎的轉移作為當前LLMs和VLMs的一個基本限制。

##### **From Skill Text to Skill Structure: The Scheduling-Structural-Logical Representation for Agent Skills**
2604.24026v2 by Qiliang Liang, Hansi Wang, Zhong Liang, Yang Liu

LLM agents increasingly rely on reusable skills, capability packages that combine instructions, control flow, constraints, and tool calls. In most current agent systems, however, skills are still represented by text-heavy artifacts, including SKILL{.}md-style documents and structured records whose machine-usable evidence remains embedded largely in natural-language descriptions. This poses a challenge for skill-centered agent systems: managing skill collections and using skills to support agent both require reasoning over invocation interfaces, execution structure, and concrete side effects that are often entangled in a single textual surface. An explicit representation of skill knowledge may therefore help make these artifacts easier for machines to acquire and leverage. Drawing on Memory Organization Packets, Script Theory, and Conceptual Dependency from Schank and Abelson's classical work on linguistic knowledge representation, we introduce what is, to our knowledge, the first structured representation for agent skill artifacts that disentangles skill-level scheduling signals, scene-level execution structure, and logic-level action and resource-use evidence: the Scheduling-Structural-Logical (SSL) representation. We instantiate SSL with an LLM-based normalizer and evaluate it on a corpus of skills in two tasks, Skill Discovery and Risk Assessment, and superiorly outperform the text-only baselines: in Skill Discovery, SSL improves MRR from 0.573 to 0.707; in Risk Assessment, it improves macro F1 from 0.744 to 0.787. These findings reveal that explicit, source-grounded structure makes agent skills easier to search and review. They also suggest that SSL is best understood as a practical step toward more inspectable, reusable, and operationally actionable skill representations for agent systems, rather than as a finished standard or an end-to-end mechanism for managing and using skills.

摘要：LLM 代理越來越依賴可重用的技能，這些技能包結合了指令、控制流程、約束和工具調用。然而，在大多數當前的代理系統中，技能仍然以文本為主的工件來表示，包括 SKILL{.}md 風格的文檔和結構化記錄，其機器可用的證據仍然主要嵌入在自然語言描述中。這對以技能為中心的代理系統提出了挑戰：管理技能集合和使用技能來支持代理都需要對調用介面、執行結構和具體副作用進行推理，而這些通常糾纏在單一的文本表面中。因此，技能知識的明確表示可能有助於使這些工件更容易被機器獲取和利用。基於記憶組織包、腳本理論以及 Schank 和 Abelson 在語言知識表示方面的經典工作中的概念依賴，我們介紹了我們所知的第一個結構化表示，用於代理技能工件，該表示解開了技能級調度信號、場景級執行結構和邏輯級行動及資源使用證據：調度-結構-邏輯 (SSL) 表示。我們用基於 LLM 的標準化器實現了 SSL，並在兩個任務的技能語料庫上進行評估，分別是技能發現和風險評估，並在性能上優於僅文本基準：在技能發現中，SSL 將 MRR 從 0.573 提高到 0.707；在風險評估中，將宏觀 F1 從 0.744 提高到 0.787。這些發現揭示了明確的、基於來源的結構使代理技能更容易搜索和審查。它們還表明，SSL 最好被理解為朝向更可檢查、可重用和可操作的技能表示的實際一步，而不是作為一個完成的標準或端到端的機制來管理和使用技能。

##### **Propagation Structure-Semantic Transfer Learning for Robust Fake News Detection**
2604.23974v1 by Mengyang Chen, Lingwei Wei, Han Cao, Wei Zhou, Zhou Yan, Songlin Hu

Fake news generally refers to false information that is spread deliberately to deceive people, which has detrimental social effects. Existing fake news detection methods primarily learn the semantic features from news content or integrate structural features from propagation. However, in practical scenarios, due to the semantic ambiguity of informal language and unreliable user interactive behaviors on social media, there are inherent semantic and structural noises in news content and propagation. Although some recent works consider the effect of irrelevant user interactions in a hybrid-modeling way, they still suffer from the mutual interference between structural noise and semantic noise, leading to limited performance for robust detection. To alleviate this issue, this paper proposes a novel Propagation Structure-Semantic Transfer Learning framework (PSS-TL) for robust fake news detection under a teacher-student architecture. Specifically, we design dual teacher models to learn semantics knowledge and structure knowledge from noisy news content and propagation structure independently. Besides, we design a Multi-channel Knowledge Distillation (MKD) loss to enable the student model to acquire specialized knowledge from the teacher models, thereby avoiding mutual interference. Extensive experiments on two real-world datasets validate the effectiveness and robustness of our method.

摘要：假新聞通常指的是故意散播的虛假信息，以欺騙人們，這對社會造成了有害的影響。現有的假新聞檢測方法主要從新聞內容中學習語義特徵或整合來自傳播的結構特徵。然而，在實際場景中，由於非正式語言的語義模糊性和社交媒體上不可靠的用戶互動行為，新聞內容和傳播中存在固有的語義和結構噪聲。儘管一些近期的研究以混合建模的方式考慮了無關用戶互動的影響，但它們仍然受到結構噪聲和語義噪聲之間的相互干擾，導致穩健檢測的性能有限。為了緩解這一問題，本文提出了一種新穎的傳播結構-語義轉移學習框架（PSS-TL），用於在教師-學生架構下進行穩健的假新聞檢測。具體而言，我們設計了雙教師模型，獨立地從噪聲新聞內容和傳播結構中學習語義知識和結構知識。此外，我們設計了一種多通道知識蒸餾（MKD）損失，以使學生模型能夠從教師模型中獲取專門知識，從而避免相互干擾。在兩個真實世界數據集上的大量實驗驗證了我們方法的有效性和穩健性。

##### **Quantum Knowledge Graph: Modeling Context-Dependent Triplet Validity**
2604.23972v1 by Yao Wang, Zixu Geng, Jun Yan

Knowledge graphs (KGs) are increasingly used to support large lan guage model (LLM) reasoning, but standard triplet-based KGs treat each relation as globally valid. In many settings, whether a relation should count as evidence depends on the context. We therefore formulate triplet validity as a triplet-specific function of context and refer to this formulation as a Quantum Knowledge Graph (QKG). We instantiate QKG in medicine using a diabetes-centered PrimeKG subgraph, whose 68,651 context-sensitive relations are further annotated with patient-group-specific constraints. We evaluate it in a reasoner--validator pipeline for medical question answering on a KG-grounded subset of MedReason containing 2,788 questions. With Haiku-4.5 as both the Reasoner and the Validator, KG-backed validation significantly improves over a no-validator baseline ($+0.61$ pp), and QKG with context matching yields the largest gain, outperforming both KG validation without context matching ($+0.79$ pp) and the no-validator baseline ($+1.40$ pp; paired McNemar, all $p<0.05$). Under a stronger validator (Qwen-3.6-Plus), the raw QKG gain over the no-validator baseline grows from $+1.40$ pp to $+5.96$ pp; the context-matching gap is non-significant ($p=0.73$) on the raw set but becomes borderline significant ($p=0.05$) after adjustment for knowledge leakage and suspicious questions, consistent with a benchmark-gold ceiling rather than a QKG limitation. Taken together, the results support the view that the value of a KG in LLM-based clinical reasoning lies not merely in storing medically related facts, but in representing whether those facts are applicable to the specific patient context. For reproducibility and further research, we release the curated QKG datasets and source code.\footnote{https://github.com/HKAI-Sci/QKG}

摘要：知識圖譜（KGs）越來越多地用於支持大型語言模型（LLM）的推理，但標準的基於三元組的KGs將每個關係視為全局有效。在許多情境中，某個關係是否應該被視為證據取決於上下文。因此，我們將三元組的有效性表述為一個特定於三元組的上下文函數，並將這一表述稱為量子知識圖譜（QKG）。我們在醫學中實現QKG，使用以糖尿病為中心的PrimeKG子圖，其68,651個上下文敏感的關係進一步附加了特定於患者群體的約束。我們在一個推理者-驗證者管道中對其進行評估，針對KG基礎的MedReason子集進行醫學問題回答，該子集包含2,788個問題。使用Haiku-4.5作為推理者和驗證者，KG支持的驗證顯著改善了無驗證者基線（$+0.61$ pp），而具有上下文匹配的QKG則產生了最大的增益，超越了沒有上下文匹配的KG驗證（$+0.79$ pp）和無驗證者基線（$+1.40$ pp；配對McNemar，所有$p&lt;0.05$）。在一個更強的驗證者（Qwen-3.6-Plus）下，原始QKG相對於無驗證者基線的增益從$+1.40$ pp增長到$+5.96$ pp；在原始數據集上，上下文匹配的差距不顯著（$p=0.73$），但在調整知識洩露和可疑問題後變得邊際顯著（$p=0.05$），這與基準金標準上限一致，而不是QKG的限制。綜合來看，結果支持這樣的觀點：KG在基於LLM的臨床推理中的價值不僅在於存儲醫學相關事實，還在於表示這些事實是否適用於特定的患者上下文。為了可重複性和進一步研究，我們釋放了經過策劃的QKG數據集和源代碼。\footnote{https://github.com/HKAI-Sci/QKG}

##### **LLM-Guided Agentic Floor Plan Parsing for Accessible Indoor Navigation of Blind and Low-Vision People**
2604.23970v1 by Aydin Ayanzadeh, Tim Oates

Indoor navigation remains a critical accessibility challenge for the blind and low-vision (BLV) individuals, as existing solutions rely on costly per-building infrastructure. We present an agentic framework that converts a single floor plan image into a structured, retrievable knowledge base to generate safe, accessible navigation instructions with lightweight infrastructure. The system has two phases: a multi-agent module that parses the floor plan into a spatial knowledge graph through a self-correcting pipeline with iterative retry loops and corrective feedback; and a Path Planner that generates accessible navigation instructions, with a Safety Evaluator agent assessing potential hazards along each route. We evaluate the system on the real-world UMBC Math and Psychology building (floors MP-1 and MP-3) and on the CVC-FP benchmark. On MP-1, we achieve success rates of 92.31%, 76.92%, and 61.54% for short, medium, and long routes, outperforming the strongest single-call baseline (Claude 3.7 Sonnet) at 84.62%, 69.23%, and 53.85%. On MP-3, we reach 76.92%, 61.54%, and 38.46%, compared to the best baseline at 61.54%, 46.15%, and 23.08%. These results show consistent gains over single-call LLM baselines and demonstrate that our workflow is a scalable solution for accessible indoor navigation for BLV individuals.

摘要：室內導航對盲人和低視力（BLV）個體來說仍然是一個關鍵的可及性挑戰，因為現有的解決方案依賴於昂貴的每棟建築基礎設施。<lb/>我們提出了一個代理框架，將單一樓層平面圖像轉換為結構化的可檢索知識庫，以生成安全、可及的導航指示，並使用輕量級基礎設施。<lb/>該系統有兩個階段：一個多代理模塊，通過自我校正的管道和迭代重試循環及校正反饋，將樓層平面圖解析為空間知識圖；以及一個路徑規劃器，生成可及的導航指示，並由安全評估代理評估每條路徑上的潛在危險。<lb/>我們在現實世界的UMBC數學與心理學大樓（MP-1和MP-3樓層）以及CVC-FP基準上評估該系統。<lb/>在MP-1上，我們的成功率分別為92.31%、76.92%和61.54%，對於短、中和長路徑，超越了最強的單次調用基線（Claude 3.7 Sonnet）的84.62%、69.23%和53.85%。<lb/>在MP-3上，我們達到76.92%、61.54%和38.46%，相比之下最佳基線為61.54%、46.15%和23.08%。<lb/>這些結果顯示出相對於單次調用LLM基線的一致增長，並證明我們的工作流程是為BLV個體提供可及室內導航的可擴展解決方案。

##### **GamED.AI: A Hierarchical Multi-Agent Framework for Automated Educational Game Generation**
2604.23947v2 by Shiven Agarwal, Yash Shah, Ashish Raj Shekhar, Priyanuj Bordoloi, Vivek Gupta

We introduce GamED.AI, a hierarchical multi-agent framework that transforms instructor-provided questions into fully playable, pedagogically grounded educational games validated through formal mechanic contracts. Built on phase-based LangGraph sub-graphs, deterministic Quality Gates, and structured Pydantic schemas, GamED.AI supports two template families encompassing 15 interaction mechanics across spatial reasoning, procedural execution, and higher-order Bloom's Taxonomy objectives. Evaluated on 200 questions spanning five subject domains, the system achieves a 90% validation pass rate, 98.3% schema compliance, and 73% token reduction over ReAct agents (${\sim}$73,500 $\rightarrow$ ${\sim}$19,900 tokens/game) at $0.46 per game. Within this model configuration, these results suggest that phase-bounded architectural structure correlates more strongly with alignment quality than prompting strategy alone. Our demonstration lets attendees generate Bloom's-aligned games from natural language in under 60 seconds, inspect Quality Gate outputs at each pipeline phase, and browse a curated library of 50 games spanning all 15 mechanic types.

摘要：我們介紹 GamED.AI，一個層級多代理框架，將講師提供的問題轉換為完全可玩、以教學為基礎的教育遊戲，並通過正式的機械合約進行驗證。該框架基於基於階段的 LangGraph 子圖、確定性的質量門和結構化的 Pydantic 模式，GamED.AI 支持兩個模板系列，涵蓋 15 種互動機制，涉及空間推理、程序執行和高階布魯姆分類法目標。在涵蓋五個學科領域的 200 個問題上進行評估，該系統實現了 90% 的驗證通過率、98.3% 的模式合規性，以及相較於 ReAct 代理的 73% 令牌減少（${\sim}$73,500 $\rightarrow$ ${\sim}$19,900 tokens/game），每個遊戲的成本為 $0.46。在這種模型配置中，這些結果表明，階段限制的架構結構與對齊質量的相關性比單純的提示策略更強。我們的演示讓參與者在 60 秒內從自然語言生成與布魯姆對齊的遊戲，檢查每個管道階段的質量門輸出，並瀏覽涵蓋所有 15 種機制類型的 50 款遊戲的策展庫。

##### **Agentic AI platforms for autonomous training and rule induction of human-human and virus-human protein-protein interactions**
2604.23924v1 by Hung N. Do, Jessica Z. Kubicek-Sutherland, Oscar A. Negrete, S. Gnanakaran

We instruct an AI agent to construct two separate agentic AI platforms: one for autonomous training of predictive ML models for human-human and virus-human PPI, and the other for inducing explicit general rules governing human-human and virus-human PPI. The first agentic AI platform for autonomous training of predictive ML models for PPI is designed to consist of five AI agents that handle autonomous data collection, data verification, feature embedding, model design, and training and validation on three-way protein-disjoint cross-fold datasets. For human-human and human-virus PPIs, the final three-way protein-disjoint ensemble achieves an accuracy of 87.3% and 86.5%, respectively. For cross-checking and interpretability purposes, the second agentic AI platform is designed to replace ML predictions with human-readable rules derived from protein embeddings, physicochemical autocovariance descriptors, compartment annotations, pathway-domain overlap, and graph contexts. For human-human PPI, it is defined by a two-rule induction, whereas human-virus is induced by a more complex set of weighted rules. The rules induced by the second agentic platform align with the SHAP-identified features from the predictive ML models built by the first agentic platform. Taken together, our work demonstrates the agentic AI's ability to orchestrate from data planning to execution, and from rule induction to explanation in ML, opening the door to various applications.

摘要：我們指示一個 AI 代理構建兩個獨立的代理 AI 平台：一個用於自主訓練人類-人類和病毒-人類 PPI 的預測 ML 模型，另一個用於引導明確的通用規則，規範人類-人類和病毒-人類 PPI。第一個用於自主訓練 PPI 預測 ML 模型的代理 AI 平台設計為由五個 AI 代理組成，這些代理負責自主數據收集、數據驗證、特徵嵌入、模型設計，以及在三向蛋白質不重疊交叉折疊數據集上的訓練和驗證。對於人類-人類和人類-病毒 PPI，最終的三向蛋白質不重疊集成模型分別達到了 87.3% 和 86.5% 的準確率。為了進行交叉檢查和可解釋性目的，第二個代理 AI 平台設計為用從蛋白質嵌入、物理化學自協方差描述符、區域註釋、途徑-領域重疊和圖形上下文中派生的人類可讀規則來替代 ML 預測。對於人類-人類 PPI，它由兩條規則引導，而人類-病毒則由一組更複雜的加權規則引導。第二個代理平台引導的規則與第一個代理平台構建的預測 ML 模型中的 SHAP 識別特徵相一致。總的來說，我們的工作展示了代理 AI 從數據規劃到執行，從規則引導到 ML 解釋的能力，為各種應用開啟了大門。

##### **Knowledge Vector of Logical Reasoning in Large Language Models**
2604.23877v1 by Zixuan Wang, Yuanyuan Lei

Logical reasoning serve as a central capability in LLMs and includes three main forms: deductive, inductive, and abductive reasoning. In this work, we study the knowledge representations of these reasoning types in LLMs and analyze the correlations among them. Our analysis shows that each form of logical reasoning can be captured as a reasoning-specific knowledge vector in a linear representation space, yet these vectors are largely independent of each other. Motivated by cognitive science theory that these subforms of logical reasoning interact closely in the human brain, as well as our observation that the reasoning process for one type can benefit from the reasoning chain produced by another, we further propose to refine the knowledge representations of each reasoning type in LLMs to encourage complementarity between them. To this end, we design a complementary subspace-constrained refinement framework, which introduces a complementary loss that enables each reasoning vector to leverage auxiliary knowledge from the others, and a subspace constraint loss that prevents erasure of their unique characteristics. Through steering experiments along reasoning vectors, we find that refined vectors incorporating complementary knowledge yield consistent performance gains. We also conduct a mechanism-interpretability analysis of each reasoning vector, revealing insights into the shared and specific features of different reasoning in LLMs.

摘要：邏輯推理作為大型語言模型（LLMs）的核心能力，包括三種主要形式：演繹推理、歸納推理和溯因推理。<lb/>在本研究中，我們研究這些推理類型在LLMs中的知識表示，並分析它們之間的相關性。<lb/>我們的分析顯示，每種邏輯推理形式都可以在線性表示空間中被捕捉為特定於推理的知識向量，但這些向量彼此之間大體上是獨立的。<lb/>受到認知科學理論的啟發，這些邏輯推理的子形式在人的大腦中密切互動，以及我們觀察到一種類型的推理過程可以受益於另一種類型產生的推理鏈，我們進一步提出在LLMs中細化每種類型的知識表示，以促進它們之間的互補性。<lb/>為此，我們設計了一個互補子空間約束的細化框架，該框架引入了一種互補損失，使每個推理向量能夠利用來自其他向量的輔助知識，並引入一種子空間約束損失，以防止其獨特特徵的消失。<lb/>通過沿著推理向量進行引導實驗，我們發現 incorporating 互補知識的細化向量產生了一致的性能提升。<lb/>我們還對每個推理向量進行了機制可解釋性分析，揭示了LLMs中不同推理的共享和特定特徵的見解。

##### **Graph Memory Transformer (GMT)**
2604.23862v1 by Nicola Zanarini, Niccolò Ferrari

We investigate whether the Feed-Forward Network (FFN) sublayer in a decoder-only transformer can be replaced by an explicit learned memory graph while preserving the surrounding autoregressive architecture. The proposed Graph Memory Transformer (GMT) keeps causal self-attention intact, but replaces the usual per-token FFN transformation with a memory cell that routes token representations over a learned bank of centroids connected by a learned directed transition matrix. In the base GMT v7 instantiation studied here, each of 16 transformer blocks contains 128 centroids, a 128 * 128 edge matrix, gravitational source routing, token-conditioned target selection, and a gated displacement readout. The cell therefore returns movement from an estimated source memory state toward a target memory state, rather than a retrieved value. The resulting model is a fully decoder-only language model with 82.2M trainable parameters and no dense FFN sublayers, compared with a 103.0M-parameter dense GPT-style baseline used in the evaluation. The base v7 model trains stably and exposes centroid usage, transition structure, and source-to-target movement as directly inspectable quantities of the forward computation. It remains behind the larger dense baseline in validation loss and perplexity (3.5995/36.58 vs. 3.2903/26.85), while showing close zero-shot benchmark behavior under the evaluated setting. These results are not intended as a state-of-the-art claim; they support the viability and structural interpretability of replacing dense within-token transformation with graph-mediated memory navigation. Broader scaling, optimized kernels, and more extensive benchmark evaluation are left for subsequent work.

摘要：我們調查了在僅解碼器的Transformer中，前饋網絡（FFN）子層是否可以被明確學習的記憶圖所取代，同時保持周圍的自回歸架構。所提出的圖記憶Transformer（GMT）保持因果自注意力不變，但用一個記憶單元取代了通常的每個標記的FFN變換，該記憶單元通過一個學習的有向轉移矩陣將標記表示路由到一個學習的質心庫。這裡研究的基礎GMT v7實例中，每個16個Transformer塊包含128個質心、一個128 * 128的邊緣矩陣、重力源路由、標記條件目標選擇和一個門控位移讀出。因此，該單元返回從估計的源記憶狀態向目標記憶狀態的運動，而不是檢索的值。與在評估中使用的103.0M參數的密集GPT風格基線相比，所得到的模型是一個完全的僅解碼器語言模型，擁有82.2M可訓練參數，且沒有密集的FFN子層。基礎v7模型穩定訓練，並將質心使用、轉移結構和源到目標的運動暴露為可直接檢查的前向計算量。它在驗證損失和困惑度上仍落後於更大的密集基線（3.5995/36.58對比3.2903/26.85），同時在評估設置下顯示出接近零樣本基準行為。這些結果並不旨在作為最先進的聲明；它們支持用圖介導的記憶導航取代密集的內部標記變換的可行性和結構可解釋性。更廣泛的擴展、優化內核和更廣泛的基準評估將留待後續工作。

##### **Scalable Production Scheduling: Linear Complexity via Unified Homogeneous Graphs**
2604.23841v1 by Jonathan Hoss, Moritz Link, Noah Klarmann

Efficiently solving the Job Shop Scheduling Problem in real-world industrial applications requires policies that are both computationally lean and topologically robust. While Reinforcement Learning has shown potential in automating dispatching rules, existing models often struggle with a scalability bottleneck caused by quadratic graph complexity or the architectural overhead of heterogeneous layers. We introduce a unified graph framework that employs feature-based homogenization to project distinct node roles into a shared latent space. This allows a standard homogeneous Graph Isomorphism Network to capture complex resource contention with linear complexity, ensuring low-latency inference for large-scale industrial applications. Our empirical results demonstrate that our framework achieves state-of-the-art performance while exhibiting consistent zero-shot generalization. We identify the job-to-machine ratio as the primary driver of policy effectiveness, rather than absolute problem size. Based on this, we propose a hypothesis of structural saturation, demonstrating that policies trained on critically congested instances ($\mathcal{J} \approx \mathcal{M}$) learn scale-invariant resolution strategies. Agents trained at this saturation point internalize invariant conflict-resolution logic, allowing them to treat massive rectangular instances as a sequential concatenation of saturated sub-problems. This approach eliminates the need for expensive scale-specific retraining and prevents overfitting to statistical shortcuts, providing a robust and efficient pathway for deploying RL solutions in dynamic production environments.

摘要：有效解決實際工業應用中的工作車間排程問題需要既計算高效又拓撲穩健的政策。雖然強化學習在自動化調度規則方面顯示出潛力，但現有模型往往面臨由於二次圖形複雜性或異構層的架構開銷造成的可擴展性瓶頸。我們提出了一個統一的圖形框架，利用基於特徵的同質化將不同的節點角色投影到共享的潛在空間。這使得標準的同質圖同構網絡能以線性複雜度捕捉複雜的資源競爭，確保在大規模工業應用中進行低延遲推斷。我們的實證結果表明，我們的框架實現了最先進的性能，同時展現出一致的零樣本泛化。我們確定工作與機器的比例是政策有效性的主要驅動因素，而不是絕對問題大小。基於此，我們提出了一個結構飽和的假設，證明在臨界擁擠實例上訓練的政策（$\mathcal{J} \approx \mathcal{M}$）學會了尺度不變的解決策略。在這個飽和點訓練的代理內化了不變的衝突解決邏輯，使他們能將大規模矩形實例視為飽和子問題的序列串聯。這種方法消除了對昂貴的特定規模再訓練的需求，並防止了對統計捷徑的過擬合，為在動態生產環境中部署強化學習解決方案提供了一條穩健而高效的途徑。

##### **Domain-Filtered Knowledge Graphs from Sparse Autoencoder Features**
2604.23829v2 by John Winnicki, Abeynaya Gnanasekaran, Eric Darve

Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) extract millions of interpretable features from a language model, but flat feature inventories aren't very useful on their own. Domain concepts get mixed with generic and weakly grounded features, while related ideas are scattered across many units, and there's no way to understand relationships between features. We address this by first constructing a strict domain-specific concept universe from a large SAE inventory using contrastive activations and a multi-stage filtering process. Next, we build two aligned graph views on the filtered set: a co-occurrence graph for corpus-level conceptual structure, organized at multiple levels of granularity, and a transcoder-based mechanism graph that links source-layer and target-layer features through sparse latent pathways. Automated edge labeling then turns these graph views into readable knowledge graphs rather than unlabeled layouts. In a case study on a biology textbook, these graphs recover coherent chapter and subchapter-level structure, reveal concepts that bridge neighboring topics, and transform messy sentence-level activity containing thousands of features into compact, readable views that illustrate the model's local activity. Taken together, this reframes a flat SAE inventory as an internal knowledge graph that converts feature-level interpretability into a global map of model knowledge and enables audits of reasoning faithfulness.

摘要：稀疏自編碼器（SAEs）從語言模型中提取數百萬個可解釋的特徵，但平坦的特徵庫本身並不太有用。領域概念與一般性和弱基礎的特徵混合在一起，而相關的想法則散布在許多單元中，沒有辦法理解特徵之間的關係。我們通過首先使用對比激活和多階段過濾過程，從大型SAE庫構建一個嚴格的領域特定概念宇宙來解決這個問題。接下來，我們在過濾後的集合上構建兩個對齊的圖視圖：一個用於語料庫級概念結構的共現圖，按多個粒度級別組織，以及一個基於轉碼器的機制圖，通過稀疏潛在通道將源層和目標層特徵連接起來。自動邊緣標籤化隨後將這些圖視圖轉換為可讀的知識圖，而不是未標記的佈局。在一項針對生物學教科書的案例研究中，這些圖恢復了連貫的章節和子章節級結構，揭示了橋接相鄰主題的概念，並將包含數千個特徵的雜亂句子級活動轉換為緊湊、可讀的視圖，展示模型的局部活動。綜合來看，這將平坦的SAE庫重新構架為一個內部知識圖，將特徵級的可解釋性轉換為模型知識的全球地圖，並使推理的忠實性審計成為可能。

##### **Domain Fine-Tuning vs. Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Medical Multiple-Choice Question Answering: A Controlled Comparison at the 4B-Parameter Scale**
2604.23801v1 by Avi-ad Avraam Buskila

Practitioners deploying small open-weight large language models (LLMs) for medical question answering face a recurring design choice: invest in a domain-fine-tuned model, or keep a general-purpose model and inject domain knowledge at inference time via retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). We isolate this trade-off by holding model size, prompt template, decoding temperature, retrieval pipeline, and evaluation protocol fixed, and varying only (i) whether the model has been domain-adapted (Gemma 3 4B vs. MedGemma 4B, both 4-bit quantized and served via Ollama) and (ii) whether retrieved passages from a medical knowledge corpus are inserted into the prompt. We evaluate all four cells of this 2x2 design on the full MedQA-USMLE 4-option test split (1,273 questions) with three repetitions per question (15,276 LLM calls). Domain fine-tuning yields a +6.8 percentage-point gain in majority-vote accuracy over the general 4B baseline (53.3% vs. 46.4%, McNemar p < 10^-4). RAG over MedMCQA explanations does not produce a statistically significant gain in either model, and in the domain-tuned model the point estimate is slightly negative (-1.9 pp, p = 0.16). At this scale and on this benchmark, domain knowledge encoded in weights dominates domain knowledge supplied in context. We release the full experiment code and JSONL traces to support replication.

摘要：從事小型開放權重大型語言模型（LLMs）用於醫學問題回答的實踐者面臨一個反覆出現的設計選擇：投資於一個領域微調的模型，還是保留一個通用模型並在推理時通過檢索增強生成（RAG）注入領域知識。<lb/>我們通過固定模型大小、提示模板、解碼溫度、檢索管道和評估協議，並僅變化（i）模型是否經過領域適應（Gemma 3 4B 與 MedGemma 4B，均為 4 位元量化並通過 Ollama 提供服務）以及（ii）是否將來自醫學知識語料庫的檢索段落插入提示中，來隔離這一權衡。<lb/>我們在完整的 MedQA-USMLE 4 選項測試拆分（1,273 個問題）上評估這個 2x2 設計的四個單元，每個問題重複三次（15,276 次 LLM 調用）。<lb/>領域微調相對於一般的 4B 基線（53.3% 對 46.4%，McNemar p < 10^-4）帶來了 +6.8 個百分點的多數投票準確率增益。<lb/>在兩個模型中，對 MedMCQA 解釋的 RAG 並未產生統計上顯著的增益，而在領域微調的模型中，點估計略為負值（-1.9 pp，p = 0.16）。<lb/>在這個規模和這個基準下，編碼在權重中的領域知識主導了在上下文中提供的領域知識。<lb/>我們發布完整的實驗代碼和 JSONL 跟蹤，以支持重複實驗。

##### **The Override Gap: A Magnitude Account of Knowledge Conflict Failure in Hypernetwork-Based Instant LLM Adaptation**
2604.23750v1 by Shuaizhi Cheng, Xiang Shi, Mingwei Li

Hypernetwork-based methods such as Doc-to-LoRA internalize a document into an LLM's weights in a single forward pass, but they fail systematically on conflicts: when the document contradicts pretraining knowledge, accuracy collapses to 46.4% on the deepest facts. We show the failure is a magnitude problem rather than a representational one. The hypernetwork already targets the right layers, but its adapter margin is approximately constant across documents while the pretrained margin grows with training frequency, so deep conflicts lose by construction. The account predicts that failure should track prior strength: sorting 194 conflicts by the base model's log-probability on the contradicted fact, baseline accuracy falls from 68% on weak-prior questions to 16% on strong-prior ones, a 52 percentage-point gap. The cure is amplitude. Selective Layer Boosting scales the adapter at its top-norm layers, and Conflict-Aware Internalization triggers boosting only when the base model is confident. Both are training-free; together they raise deep-conflict accuracy from 46.4% to 71.0% on Gemma-2B and from 53.6% to 72.5% on Mistral-7B while preserving novel-knowledge recall, and beat vanilla retrieval-augmented generation on medium conflicts by 18 percentage points despite operating entirely in parameter space. We release KID-Bench, a 489-question benchmark that separates novel recall, cross-knowledge combination, and prior-graded conflicts.

摘要：基於超網絡的方法，如 Doc-to-LoRA，將文檔內化到 LLM 的權重中，僅需一次前向傳遞，但在衝突上系統性失敗：當文檔與預訓練知識相矛盾時，對於最深的事實，準確率降至 46.4%。我們顯示這一失敗是幅度問題，而非表徵問題。超網絡已經針對正確的層，但其適配器邊際在不同文檔之間大致保持不變，而預訓練邊際隨著訓練頻率的增長而增長，因此深層衝突在結構上會失敗。該解釋預測失敗應該與先前的強度相關：根據基礎模型在被矛盾事實上的對數概率對 194 個衝突進行排序，基準準確率從弱先驗問題的 68% 降至強先驗問題的 16%，相差 52 個百分點。解決方案是幅度。選擇性層增強在其頂部規範層上擴展適配器，而衝突感知內化僅在基礎模型有信心時啟動增強。這兩者都是無需訓練的；它們共同將深層衝突的準確率從 46.4% 提升至 71.0%（Gemma-2B），並將 Mistral-7B 的準確率從 53.6% 提升至 72.5%，同時保持新知識的回憶，並在中等衝突中比原始檢索增強生成高出 18 個百分點，儘管完全在參數空間中運作。我們發布了 KID-Bench，一個包含 489 個問題的基準，區分新穎回憶、跨知識組合和先驗分級衝突。

##### **Expert Evaluation of LLM's Open-Ended Legal Reasoning on the Japanese Bar Exam Writing Task**
2604.23730v1 by Jungmin Choi, Keisuke Sakaguchi, Hiroaki Yamada

Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong performance on legal benchmarks, including multiple-choice components of bar exams. However, their capacity for generating open-ended legal reasoning in realistic scenarios remains insufficiently explored. Notably, to our best knowledge, there are no prior studies or datasets addressing this issue in the Japanese context.
  This study presents the first dataset designed to evaluate the open-ended legal reasoning performance of LLMs within the Japanese jurisdiction. The dataset is based on the writing component of the Japanese bar examination, which requires examinees to identify multiple legal issues from long narratives and to construct structured legal arguments in free text format. Our key contribution is the manual evaluation of LLMs' generated responses by legal experts, which reveals limitations and challenges in legal reasoning. Moreover, we conducted a manual analysis of hallucinations to characterize when and how the models introduce content not supported by precedent or law.
  Our real exam questions, model-generated responses, and expert evaluations reveal the milestones of current LLMs in the Japanese legal domain. Our dataset and relevant resources will be available online.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在法律基準上表現出色，包括律師考試的多選題部分。然而，它們在現實情境中生成開放式法律推理的能力仍然未被充分探索。值得注意的是，據我們所知，沒有先前的研究或數據集在日本背景下解決這個問題。<lb/>本研究提出了第一個旨在評估LLMs在日本法域內開放式法律推理表現的數據集。該數據集基於日本律師考試的寫作部分，要求考生從長篇敘述中識別多個法律問題，並以自由文本格式構建結構化法律論證。我們的主要貢獻是由法律專家對LLMs生成的回應進行手動評估，這揭示了法律推理中的局限性和挑戰。此外，我們對幻覺進行了手動分析，以描述模型何時以及如何引入不受先例或法律支持的內容。<lb/>我們的真實考試問題、模型生成的回應和專家評估揭示了當前LLMs在日本法律領域的里程碑。我們的數據集和相關資源將在線上提供。

#### Abstracts
##### **Turning the TIDE: Cross-Architecture Distillation for Diffusion Large Language Models**
2604.26951v1 by Gongbo Zhang, Wen Wang, Ye Tian, Li Yuan

Diffusion large language models (dLLMs) offer parallel decoding and bidirectional context, but state-of-the-art dLLMs require billions of parameters for competitive performance. While existing distillation methods for dLLMs reduce inference steps within a single architecture, none address cross-architecture knowledge transfer, in which the teacher and student differ in architecture, attention mechanism, and tokenizer. We present TIDE, the first framework for cross-architecture dLLM distillation, comprising three modular components: (1) TIDAL, which jointly modulates distillation strength across training progress and diffusion timestep to account for the teacher's noise-dependent reliability; (2) CompDemo, which enriches the teacher's context via complementary mask splitting to improve predictions under heavy masking; and (3) Reverse CALM, a cross-tokenizer objective that inverts chunk-level likelihood matching, yielding bounded gradients and dual-end noise filtering. Distilling 8B dense and 16B MoE teachers into a 0.6B student via two heterogeneous pipelines outperforms the baseline by an average of 1.53 points across eight benchmarks, yielding notable gains in code generation, where HumanEval scores reach 48.78 compared to 32.3 for the AR baseline.

摘要：擴散大型語言模型（dLLMs）提供平行解碼和雙向上下文，但最先進的 dLLMs 需要數十億的參數以達到競爭性能。雖然現有的 dLLMs 蒸餾方法在單一架構內減少推理步驟，但沒有一種方法能解決跨架構知識轉移的問題，其中教師和學生在架構、注意力機制和標記器上有所不同。我們提出了 TIDE，第一個跨架構 dLLM 蒸餾框架，包含三個模組化組件：（1）TIDAL，該組件在訓練進展和擴散時間步驟中共同調節蒸餾強度，以考慮教師的噪聲依賴可靠性；（2）CompDemo，通過互補的掩碼分割來豐富教師的上下文，以改善在重度掩碼下的預測；以及（3）Reverse CALM，一個跨標記器的目標，反轉塊級似然匹配，產生有界梯度和雙端噪聲過濾。通過兩個異質管道將 8B 密集和 16B MoE 教師蒸餾為 0.6B 學生，在八個基準測試中平均超越基準 1.53 分，在代碼生成方面獲得顯著增益，其中 HumanEval 分數達到 48.78，相較於 AR 基準的 32.3。

##### **Select to Think: Unlocking SLM Potential with Local Sufficiency**
2604.26940v1 by Wenxuan Ye, Yangyang Zhang, Xueli An, Georg Carle, Yunpu Ma

Small language models (SLMs) offer computational efficiency for scalable deployment, yet they often fall short of the reasoning power exhibited by their larger counterparts (LLMs). To mitigate this gap, current approaches invoke an LLM to generate tokens at points of reasoning divergence, but these external calls introduce substantial latency and costs. Alternatively, standard distillation is often hindered by the capacity limitation, as SLMs struggle to accurately mimic the LLM's complex generative distribution. We address this dilemma by identifying local sufficiency: at divergence points, the LLM's preferred token consistently resides within the SLM's top-K next-token predictions, even when failing to emerge as the SLM top-1 choice. We therefore propose SELECT TO THINK (S2T), which reframes the LLM's role from open-ended generation to selection among the SLM's proposals, simplifying the supervision signal to discrete candidate rankings. Leveraging this, we introduce S2T-LOCAL, which distills the selection logic into the SLM, empowering it to perform autonomous re-ranking without inference-time LLM dependency. Empirically, we demonstrate that a 1.5B SLM's top-8 candidates capture the 32B LLM's choice with 95% hit rate. Translating this potential into performance, S2T-LOCAL improves greedy decoding by 24.1% on average across benchmarks, effectively matching the efficacy of 8-path self-consistency while operating with single-trajectory efficiency.

摘要：小型語言模型（SLMs）在可擴展部署方面提供了計算效率，但它們在推理能力上往往不及其較大的對應模型（LLMs）。為了減少這一差距，當前的方法在推理分歧點調用LLM生成標記，但這些外部調用會引入顯著的延遲和成本。另一方面，標準蒸餾常常受到容量限制的阻礙，因為SLMs難以準確模仿LLM的複雜生成分佈。我們通過識別局部充分性來解決這一困境：在分歧點，LLM的首選標記始終位於SLM的前K個下一標記預測中，即使它未能成為SLM的首選。我們因此提出了SELECT TO THINK（S2T），這將LLM的角色從開放式生成重新構建為在SLM的提議中進行選擇，簡化了監督信號為離散候選排名。利用這一點，我們引入了S2T-LOCAL，將選擇邏輯蒸餾到SLM中，使其能夠在不依賴推理時LLM的情況下進行自主重新排序。在實證上，我們證明了一個15億參數的SLM的前8個候選項以95%的命中率捕捉了320億參數LLM的選擇。將這一潛力轉化為性能，S2T-LOCAL在各基準測試中平均提高了24.1%的貪婪解碼效果，有效匹配了8路自一致性的效能，同時以單一軌跡的效率運行。

##### **ClassEval-Pro: A Cross-Domain Benchmark for Class-Level Code Generation**
2604.26923v1 by Yeheng Chen, Chaoxiang Xie, Yuling Shi, Wenhao Zeng, Yongpan Wang, Hongyu Zhang, Xiaodong Gu

LLMs have achieved strong results on both function-level code synthesis and repository-level code modification, yet a capability that falls between these two extremes -- compositional code creation, i.e., building a complete, internally structured class from a specification -- remains underserved. Current evaluations are either confined to isolated functions or rely on manually curated class-level tasks that are expensive to scale and increasingly susceptible to data contamination. We introduce ClassEval-Pro, a benchmark of 300 class-level tasks spanning 11 domains, constructed through an automated three-stage pipeline that combines complexity enhancement, cross-domain class composition, and integration of real-world GitHub code contributed after January 2025. Every task is validated by an LLM Judge Ensemble and must pass test suites with over 90% line coverage. We evaluate five frontier LLMs under five generation strategies. The best model achieves only 45.6% class-level Pass@1, with a 17.7-point gap between the strongest and weakest models, confirming the benchmark's discriminative power. Strategy choice strongly interacts with model capability: structured approaches such as bottom-up improve weaker models by up to 9.4 percentage points, while compositional generation collapses to as low as 1.3%. Error analysis over 500 manually annotated failures reveals that logic errors (56.2%) and dependency errors (38.0%) dominate, identifying cross-method coordination as the core bottleneck.

摘要：LLMs 在功能級別的代碼合成和庫級別的代碼修改方面取得了強勁的成果，但介於這兩者之間的能力——組合代碼創建，即從規範構建一個完整的、內部結構化的類——仍然得不到充分的重視。當前的評估要麼僅限於孤立的函數，要麼依賴於手動策劃的類級任務，這些任務在擴展時成本高昂，且越來越容易受到數據污染的影響。我們介紹了 ClassEval-Pro，一個涵蓋 11 個領域的 300 個類級任務的基準，這些任務是通過一個自動化的三階段流程構建的，該流程結合了複雜性增強、跨領域類組合和整合 2025 年 1 月之後貢獻的現實世界 GitHub 代碼。每個任務都經過 LLM 評判團的驗證，並必須通過超過 90% 行覆蓋率的測試套件。我們在五種生成策略下評估了五個前沿 LLM。最佳模型的類級 Pass@1 僅達 45.6%，最強和最弱模型之間的差距為 17.7 個百分點，證實了基準的區分能力。策略選擇與模型能力之間存在強烈的互動：結構化方法如自下而上可使較弱的模型提升最多 9.4 個百分點，而組合生成則低至 1.3%。對 500 個手動標註的失敗案例的錯誤分析顯示，邏輯錯誤（56.2%）和依賴錯誤（38.0%）占主導地位，識別出跨方法協調是核心瓶頸。

##### **Causal Learning with Neural Assemblies**
2604.26919v1 by Evangelia Kopadi, Dimitris Kalles

Can Neural Assemblies -- groups of neurons that fire together and strengthen through co-activation -- learn the direction of causal influence between variables? While established as a computationally general substrate for classification, parsing, and planning, neural assemblies have not yet been shown to internalize causal directionality. We demonstrate that the inherent operations of neural assemblies -- projection, local plasticity control, and sparse winner selection -- are sufficient for directional learning. We introduce DIRECT (DIRectional Edge Coupling/Training), a mechanism that co-activates source and target assemblies under an adaptive gain schedule to internalize directed relations. Unlike backpropagation-based methods, DIRECT relies solely on local plasticity, making the resulting causal claims auditable at the mechanism level. Our findings are verified through a dual-readout validation strategy: (i) synaptic-strength asymmetry, measuring the emergent weight gap between forward and reverse links, and (ii) functional propagation overlap, quantifying the reliability of directional signal flow. Across multiple domains, the framework achieves perfect structural recovery under a supervised, known-structure setting. These results establish neural assemblies as an auditable bridge between biologically plausible dynamics and formal causal models, offering an "explainable by design" framework where causal claims are traceable to specific neural winners and synaptic asymmetries.

摘要：神經集合——一組共同激發並通過共同激活增強的神經元——能學習變數之間的因果影響方向嗎？雖然已被確立為分類、解析和規劃的計算通用基礎，但尚未顯示神經集合能內化因果方向性。我們證明了神經集合的固有操作——投影、本地可塑性控制和稀疏獲勝者選擇——足以進行方向性學習。我們介紹了DIRECT（DIRectional Edge Coupling/Training），這是一種在自適應增益計劃下共同激活源和目標集合的機制，以內化有向關係。與基於反向傳播的方法不同，DIRECT完全依賴於本地可塑性，使得所產生的因果主張在機制層面上可審計。我們的發現通過雙讀出驗證策略得到驗證：（i）突觸強度不對稱，測量前向和反向連接之間的突現權重差距，以及（ii）功能傳播重疊，量化方向性信號流的可靠性。在多個領域中，該框架在監督的已知結構設置下實現了完美的結構恢復。這些結果確立了神經集合作為生物學上合理的動態與正式因果模型之間的可審計橋樑，提供了一個“設計上可解釋”的框架，其中因果主張可追溯到特定的神經獲勝者和突觸不對稱性。

##### **HealthNLP_Retrievers at ArchEHR-QA 2026: Cascaded LLM Pipeline for Grounded Clinical Question Answering**
2604.26880v1 by Md Biplob Hosen, Md Alomgeer Hussein, Md Akmol Masud, Omar Faruque, Tera L Reynolds, Lujie Karen Chen

Patient portals now give individuals direct access to their electronic health records (EHRs), yet access alone does not ensure patients understand or act on the complex clinical information contained in these records. The proposed approach uses a multi-stage cascaded pipeline powered by the Gemini 2.5 Pro large language model to interpret patient-authored questions and retrieve relevant evidence from lengthy clinical notes. Across the individual tracks, the system ranked 1st in question interpretation, 5th in answer generation, 7th in evidence identification, and 9th in answer-evidence alignment. ##### **MoRFI: Monotonic Sparse Autoencoder Feature Identification**
2604.26866v1 by Dimitris Dimakopoulos, Shay B. Cohen, Ioannis Konstas

Large language models (LLMs) acquire most of their factual knowledge during the pre-training stage, through next token prediction. Subsequent stages of post-training often introduce new facts outwith the parametric knowledge, giving rise to hallucinations. While it has been demonstrated that supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on new knowledge may exacerbate the problem, the underlying mechanisms are still poorly understood. We conduct a controlled fine-tuning experiment, focusing on closed-book QA, and find latent directions that causally contribute to hallucinations. Specifically, we fine-tune Llama 3.1 8B, Gemma 2 9B and Mistral 7B v03 on seven distinct single QA datasets, controlling for the percentage of new knowledge and number of training epochs. By measuring performance on the test set, we validate that incrementally introducing new knowledge increases hallucinations, with the effect being more pronounced with prolonged training. We leverage pre-trained sparse autoencoders (SAEs) to analyze residual stream activations across various checkpoints for each model and propose Monotonic Relationship Feature Identification (MoRFI) for capturing causally relevant latents. MoRFI filters SAE features that respond monotonically to controlled fine-tuning data mixtures of a target property. Our findings show that exposure to unknown facts disrupts the model's ability to retrieve stored knowledge along a set of directions in the residual stream. Our pipeline reliably discovers them across distinct models, recovering knowledge through single-latent interventions.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在預訓練階段通過下一個標記預測獲得大部分事實知識。隨後的後訓練階段經常引入超出參數知識的新事實，導致幻覺的產生。雖然已經證明對新知識進行監督式微調（SFT）可能會加劇這個問題，但其潛在機制仍然不甚了解。我們進行了一項控制微調實驗，專注於閉卷問答，並發現潛在的方向會因果地促進幻覺的產生。具體來說，我們對 Llama 3.1 8B、Gemma 2 9B 和 Mistral 7B v03 在七個不同的單一問答數據集上進行微調，控制新知識的百分比和訓練週期的數量。通過測量測試集上的表現，我們驗證了逐步引入新知識會增加幻覺，且隨著訓練時間的延長，這一效應更加明顯。我們利用預訓練的稀疏自編碼器（SAEs）分析每個模型在各個檢查點的殘差流激活，並提出單調關係特徵識別（MoRFI）以捕捉因果相關的潛在變量。MoRFI 過濾對目標屬性的控制微調數據混合單調響應的 SAE 特徵。我們的研究結果顯示，接觸未知事實會干擾模型沿著一組方向檢索存儲知識的能力。我們的管道在不同模型中可靠地發現這些潛在變量，通過單一潛在干預恢復知識。

##### **What Kind of Language is Easy to Language-Model Under Curriculum Learning?**
2604.26844v1 by Nadine El-Naggar, Tatsuki Kuribayashi, Ted Briscoe

Many of the thousands of attested languages share common configurations of features, creating a spectrum from typologically very rare (e.g., object-verb-subject word order) or impossible languages to very common combinations of features (e.g., subject-object-verb word order). One central question is under what conditions such typological tendencies can be predicted, and specifically whether the learning bias of language models (LMs) is sufficient to reproduce such patterns. In this study, we add one dimensionality to such analysis -- the learning scenario for LMs -- to explore its interaction with the inductive bias of LMs. Specifically, as a first study, we examine the effect of curriculum learning (CL), as a developmentally motivated learning scenario, i.e., starting with simpler sentences rather than randomly-ordered input. We expand existing LM-based exploration (El-Naggar et al., 2025a,b) with a simple CL variant and find that CL substantially impacts the apparent inductive bias of LMs.

摘要：許多已證實的語言共享特徵的共同配置，形成了一個範圍，從類型學上非常罕見（例如，賓語-動詞-主語的語序）或不可能的語言到非常常見的特徵組合（例如，主語-賓語-動詞的語序）。一個核心問題是，在什麼條件下可以預測這種類型學的傾向，特別是語言模型（LMs）的學習偏見是否足以重現這些模式。在這項研究中，我們為這種分析增加了一個維度——LM的學習場景——以探討其與LM的歸納偏見之間的互動。具體而言，作為第一項研究，我們檢查課程學習（CL）的效果，作為一種發展性驅動的學習場景，即從較簡單的句子開始，而不是隨機排序的輸入。我們用一個簡單的CL變體擴展了現有的基於LM的探索（El-Naggar et al., 2025a,b），並發現CL對LM的明顯歸納偏見有顯著影響。

##### **Language Diffusion Models are Associative Memories Capable of Retrieving Unseen Data**
2604.26841v1 by Bao Pham, Mohammed J. Zaki, Luca Ambrogioni, Dmitry Krotov, Matteo Negri

When do language diffusion models memorize their training data, and how to quantitatively assess their true generative regime? We address these questions by showing that Uniform-based Discrete Diffusion Models (UDDMs) fundamentally behave as Associative Memories (AMs) $\textit{with emergent creative capabilities}$. The core idea of an AM is to reliably recover stored data points as $\textit{memories}$ by establishing distinct basins of attraction around them. Historically, models like Hopfield networks use an explicit energy function to guarantee these stable attractors. We broaden this perspective by leveraging the observation that energy is not strictly necessary, as basins of attraction can also be formed via conditional likelihood maximization. By evaluating token recovery of $\textit{training}$ and $\textit{test}$ examples, we identify in UDDMs a sharp memorization-to-generalization transition governed by the size of the training dataset: as it increases, basins around training examples shrink and basins around unseen test examples expand, until both later converge to the same level. Crucially, we can detect this transition using only the conditional entropy of predicted token sequences: memorization is characterized by vanishing conditional entropy, while in the generalization regime the conditional entropy of most tokens remains finite. Thus, conditional entropy offers a practical probe for the memorization-to-generalization transition in deployed models.

摘要：當語言擴散模型何時會記住其訓練數據，以及如何定量評估其真正的生成模式？我們通過展示基於均勻的離散擴散模型（UDDMs）從根本上作為聯想記憶（AMs）$\textit{具備新興的創造能力}$來解決這些問題。聯想記憶的核心思想是通過在數據點周圍建立明確的吸引盆地來可靠地恢復存儲的數據點作為$\textit{記憶}$。歷史上，像霍普菲爾德網絡這樣的模型使用明確的能量函數來保證這些穩定的吸引子。我們通過利用能量並非絕對必要的觀察來擴展這一觀點，因為吸引盆地也可以通過條件似然最大化來形成。通過評估$\textit{訓練}$和$\textit{測試}$示例的標記恢復，我們在UDDMs中識別出一個由訓練數據集大小主導的記憶到泛化的明確轉變：隨著訓練數據集的增大，圍繞訓練示例的盆地縮小，而圍繞未見測試示例的盆地擴大，直到兩者最終收斂到相同的水平。關鍵是，我們可以僅使用預測標記序列的條件熵來檢測這一轉變：記憶的特徵是條件熵消失，而在泛化模式中，大多數標記的條件熵保持有限。因此，條件熵為已部署模型中的記憶到泛化轉變提供了一個實用的探測工具。

##### **Bian Que: An Agentic Framework with Flexible Skill Arrangement for Online System Operations**
2604.26805v1 by Bochao Liu, Zhipeng Qian, Yang Zhao, Xinyuan Jiang, Zihan Liang, Yufei Ma, Junpeng Zhuang, Ben Chen, Shuo Yang, Hongen Wan, Yao Wu, Chenyi Lei, Xiao Liang

Operating and maintaining (O&M) large-scale online engine systems (search, recommendation, advertising) demands substantial human effort for release monitoring, alert response, and root cause analysis. While LLM-based agents are a natural fit for these tasks, the deployment bottleneck is not reasoning capability but orchestration: selecting, for each operational event, the relevant data (metrics, logs, change events) and the applicable operational knowledge (handbook rules and practitioner experience). Feeding all signals indiscriminately causes dilution and hallucination, while manually curating the event-to-(data, knowledge) mapping is intractable under dozens of daily releases. We present Bian Que, an agentic framework with three contributions: (i) a \emph{unified operational paradigm} abstracting day-to-day O&M into three canonical patterns: release interception, proactive inspection, and alert root cause analysis; (ii) \emph{Flexible Skill Arrangement}, where each Skill specifies which data and knowledge to retrieve for a given business-module context and can be automatically generated and updated by LLMs or iteratively refined through natural-language instructions from on-call engineers; (iii) a \emph{unified self-evolving mechanism} in which one correction signal drives two parallel pathways, case-memory-to-knowledge distillation and targeted Skill refinement. Deployed on the e-commerce search engine of KuaiShou, the major short-video platform in China, Bian Que reduces alert volume by 75%, achieves 80% root-cause analysis accuracy, and cuts mean time to resolution by over 50%. Our framework achieves 99.0% pass rate on offline evaluations. Our code is available at https://github.com/benchen4395/BianQue_Assistant.

摘要：操作和維護（O&M）大規模在線引擎系統（搜索、推薦、廣告）需要大量的人力來進行版本監控、警報響應和根本原因分析。雖然基於LLM的代理非常適合這些任務，但部署瓶頸不在於推理能力，而在於協調：為每個操作事件選擇相關數據（指標、日誌、變更事件）和適用的操作知識（手冊規則和實踐經驗）。不加區別地提供所有信號會導致稀釋和幻覺，而手動策劃事件到（數據、知識）的映射在每日數十次的版本發布下是不可行的。我們提出了Bian Que，一個具有三個貢獻的代理框架：（i）一個\emph{統一操作範式}，將日常O&M抽象為三個典範模式：版本攔截、主動檢查和警報根本原因分析；（ii）\emph{靈活技能安排}，每個技能指定在給定業務模塊上下文中檢索哪些數據和知識，並可以由LLM自動生成和更新，或通過值班工程師的自然語言指令進行迭代精煉；（iii）一個\emph{統一自我演化機制}，其中一個修正信號驅動兩條平行路徑，即案例記憶到知識的蒸餾和針對性的技能精煉。部署在中國主要短視頻平台快手的電子商務搜索引擎上，Bian Que將警報量減少了75％，實現了80％的根本原因分析準確率，並將平均解決時間縮短了50％以上。我們的框架在離線評估中達到了99.0％的通過率。我們的代碼可在https://github.com/benchen4395/BianQue_Assistant獲得。

##### **Accelerating RL Post-Training Rollouts via System-Integrated Speculative Decoding**
2604.26779v1 by Hayate Iso, Tiyasa Mitra, Sudipta Mondal, Rasoul Shafipour, Venmugil Elango, Terry Kong, Yuki Huang, Seonjin Na, Izzy Putterman, Benjamin Chislett, Maor Ashkenazi, Joseph Guman, Gerald Shen, Tugrul Konuk, Ashwath Aithal, Ritika Borkar, Ran Zilberstein, Bita Rouhani

RL post-training of frontier language models is increasingly bottlenecked by autoregressive rollout generation, making rollout acceleration a central systems challenge. Many existing efficiency methods improve throughput by changing the rollout or optimization regime, for example, through off-policy execution, replay, or lower-precision generation. We study speculative decoding as a lossless acceleration primitive for RL rollouts that preserves the target model's output distribution. We implement speculative decoding in NeMo-RL with a vLLM backend, supporting both synchronous and asynchronous pipelines and enabling speculation during RL rollouts. This benefit is realizable across speculation mechanisms, such as pretrained MTP heads, small external draft models or even techniques such as Eagle3, which are traditionally applied after RL phase. This yields a deployment path for state-of-the-art speculative decoding inside RL training. In a reasoning post-training workload at 8B scale under synchronous RL, speculative decoding improves rollout throughput by 1.8x. Using a high-fidelity performance simulator, we project that combining speculative decoding with asynchronous RL yields up to 2.5x end-to-end training speedup at 235B scale.

摘要：RL後訓練的前沿語言模型越來越受到自回歸展開生成的瓶頸限制，使得展開加速成為一個核心系統挑戰。許多現有的效率方法通過改變展開或優化機制來提高吞吐量，例如，通過非策略執行、重放或低精度生成。我們研究了推測解碼作為一種無損加速原語，用於保持目標模型輸出分佈的RL展開。我們在NeMo-RL中實現了推測解碼，使用vLLM後端，支持同步和異步管道，並在RL展開期間啟用推測。這一好處可以通過各種推測機制實現，例如預訓練的MTP頭、小型外部草稿模型，甚至是傳統上在RL階段後應用的技術，如Eagle3。這為在RL訓練中內部實現最先進的推測解碼提供了一條部署路徑。在同步RL下的8B規模推理後訓練工作負載中，推測解碼將展開吞吐量提高了1.8倍。使用高保真性能模擬器，我們預測將推測解碼與異步RL結合可在235B規模下實現高達2.5倍的端到端訓練加速。

##### **MemOVCD: Training-Free Open-Vocabulary Change Detection via Cross-Temporal Memory Reasoning and Global-Local Adaptive Rectification**
2604.26774v1 by Zuzheng Kuang, Honghao Chang, Boqiang Liang, Haoqian Wang, Lijun He, Fan Li, Haixia Bi

Open-vocabulary change detection aims to identify semantic changes in bi-temporal remote sensing images without predefined categories. Recent methods combine foundation models such as SAM, DINO and CLIP, but typically process each timestamp independently or interact only at the final comparison stage. Such paradigms suffer from insufficient temporal coupling during semantic reasoning, which limits their ability to distinguish genuine semantic changes from non-semantic appearance discrepancies. In addition, patch-dominant inference on high-resolution images often weakens global semantic continuity and produces fragmented change regions. To address these issues, we propose MemOVCD, a training-free open-vocabulary change detection framework based on cross-temporal memory reasoning and global-local adaptive rectification. Specifically, we reformulate bi-temporal change detection as a two-frame tracking problem and introduce weighted bidirectional propagation to aggregate semantic evidence from both temporal directions. To stabilize memory propagation across large temporal gaps, we construct histogram-aligned transition frames to smooth abrupt appearance changes. Moreover, a global-local adaptive rectification strategy adaptively fuses local and global-view predictions, improving spatial consistency while preserving fine-grained details. Experiments on five benchmarks demonstrate that MemOVCD achieves favorable performance on two change detection tasks, validating its effectiveness and generalization under diverse open-vocabulary settings.

摘要：開放詞彙變化檢測旨在識別雙時期遙感影像中的語義變化，而無需預定義類別。最近的方法結合了基礎模型，如SAM、DINO和CLIP，但通常獨立處理每個時間戳，或僅在最終比較階段進行交互。這種範式在語義推理過程中缺乏足夠的時間耦合，限制了它們區分真正語義變化與非語義外觀差異的能力。此外，在高解析度影像上以補丁為主的推斷往往削弱了全球語義連續性，並產生了零散的變化區域。為了解決這些問題，我們提出了MemOVCD，一種基於跨時間記憶推理和全局-局部自適應修正的無需訓練的開放詞彙變化檢測框架。具體而言，我們將雙時期變化檢測重新表述為一個雙幀跟踪問題，並引入加權雙向傳播以從兩個時間方向聚合語義證據。為了穩定跨大時間間隔的記憶傳播，我們構建了直方圖對齊的過渡幀，以平滑突變的外觀變化。此外，全球-局部自適應修正策略自適應地融合了局部和全局視圖預測，提高了空間一致性，同時保留了精細的細節。在五個基準上的實驗表明，MemOVCD在兩個變化檢測任務上達到了良好的性能，驗證了其在多樣的開放詞彙設置下的有效性和泛化能力。

##### **Decoupling Knowledge and Task Subspaces for Composable Parametric Retrieval Augmented Generation**
2604.26768v1 by Weihang Su, Hanwen Zhang, Qingyao Ai, Yiqun Liu

Parametric Retrieval-Augmented Generation (PRAG) encodes external documents into lightweight parameter modules that can be retrieved and merged at inference time, offering a promising alternative to in-context retrieval augmentation. Despite its potential, many PRAG implementations train document adapters with task-supervised objectives, which may cause each adapter to encode both document-specific facts and reusable task-solving behavior. This entanglement may make adapter composition less reliable: when multiple adapters are merged at inference time, their overlapping task behaviors can accumulate together with document-specific updates, potentially making the merged adapter less stable and less focused on the intended document knowledge. To examine this issue, we explore Orthogonal Subspace Decomposition (OSD), an adapter-training setup that separates reusable task behavior from document-specific knowledge adapters. Concretely, we first train a Task LoRA to capture reusable task behavior, and then train document LoRAs to encode document-specific knowledge in a orthogonal subspace. This setup provides a controlled way to examine how orthogonalizing task and document LoRA updates affects adapter composition in multi-document PRAG. Experiments across multiple knowledge-intensive tasks and model scales suggest that this orthogonalization strategy can improve compositional robustness in parametric RAG, especially when multiple document adapters are merged.

摘要：參數檢索增強生成（PRAG）將外部文檔編碼為輕量級參數模塊，這些模塊可以在推理時被檢索和合併，提供了一種有前景的替代方案來進行上下文檢索增強。儘管其潛力巨大，許多PRAG實現使用任務監督目標訓練文檔適配器，這可能導致每個適配器同時編碼文檔特定事實和可重用的任務解決行為。這種糾纏可能使得適配器的組合不那麼可靠：當多個適配器在推理時合併時，它們重疊的任務行為可能與文檔特定的更新一起累積，從而使合併的適配器不那麼穩定，且不那麼專注於預期的文檔知識。為了檢查這個問題，我們探索了正交子空間分解（OSD），這是一種將可重用的任務行為與文檔特定知識適配器分開的適配器訓練設置。具體來說，我們首先訓練一個任務LoRA來捕捉可重用的任務行為，然後訓練文檔LoRA來在正交子空間中編碼文檔特定知識。這種設置提供了一種受控的方法來檢查正交化任務和文檔LoRA更新如何影響多文檔PRAG中的適配器組合。在多個知識密集型任務和模型規模上的實驗表明，這種正交化策略可以改善參數RAG中的組合穩健性，特別是在合併多個文檔適配器時。

##### **Domain-Adapted Small Language Models for Reliable Clinical Triage**
2604.26766v1 by Manar Aljohani, Brandon Ho, Kenneth McKinley, Dennis Ren, Xuan Wang

Accurate and consistent Emergency Severity Index (ESI) assignment remains a persistent challenge in emergency departments, where highly variable free-text triage documentation contributes to mistriage and workflow inefficiencies. This study evaluates whether open-source small language models (SLMs) can serve as reliable, privacy-preserving decision-support tools for clinical triage. We systematically compared multiple SLMs across diverse prompting pipelines and found that clinical vignettes, concise summaries of triage narratives, yielded the most accurate predictions. The SLM, Qwen2.5-7B, demonstrated the strongest balance of accuracy, stability, and computational efficiency. Through large-scale domain adaptation using expert-curated and silver-standard pediatric triage data, fine-tuned Qwen2.5-7B models substantially reduced discordance and clinically significant errors, outperforming all baseline SLMs and advanced proprietary large language models (LLMs, e.g., GPT-4o). ##### **Exploring the Potential of Probabilistic Transformer for Time Series Modeling: A Report on the ST-PT Framework**
2604.26762v1 by Zhangzhi Xiong, Haoyi Wu, You Wu, Shuqi Gu, Kan Ren, Kewei Tu

The Probabilistic Transformer (PT) establishes that the Transformer's self-attention plus its feed-forward block is mathematically equivalent to Mean-Field Variational Inference (MFVI) on a Conditional Random Field (CRF). Under this equivalence the Transformer ceases to be a black-box neural network and becomes a programmable factor graph: graph topology, factor potentials, and the message-passing schedule are all explicit and inspectable primitives that can be engineered. PT was originally developed for natural language and in this report we investigate its potential for time series. We first lift PT into the Spatial-Temporal Probabilistic Transformer (ST-PT) to repair PT's missing channel axis and weak per-step semantics, and adopt ST-PT as a shared cornerstone backbone. We then identify three distinct properties that PT/ST-PT offers as a factor-graph model and derive three Research Questions, one per property, that probe how each property can be exploited in time series: RQ1. The graph topology and potentials are direct programmable primitives. Can this be used to inject symbolic time-series priors into ST-PT through structural graph modifications, especially under data scarcity and noise? RQ2. The CRF's factor matrices are the operator's potentials. Can an external condition program these factor matrices on a per-sample basis, so that conditional generation becomes structural rather than feature-level modulation of a fixed one? RQ3. Each MFVI iteration is a Bayesian posterior update on the factor graph. Can this turn the latent transition of latent-space AutoRegressive (AR) forecasting from an opaque MLP into a principled posterior update, and can a CRF teacher distill its latents into the AR student to counter cumulative error? We give one empirical study per question. Together, these three studies position ST-PT as a programmable framework for time-series modeling.

摘要：概率Transformer（PT）確立了Transformer的自注意力加上其前饋區塊在數學上等同於條件隨機場（CRF）上的均場變分推斷（MFVI）。在這種等價性下，Transformer不再是一個黑箱神經網絡，而是成為一個可編程的因子圖：圖的拓撲、因子潛能和消息傳遞計劃都是明確且可檢查的原始元件，可以進行工程設計。PT 最初是為自然語言開發的，在本報告中，我們探討其在時間序列中的潛力。我們首先將 PT 提升為空間-時間概率Transformer（ST-PT），以修復 PT 缺失的通道軸和弱每步語義，並將 ST-PT 作為共享的基石骨幹。我們然後確定了 PT/ST-PT 作為因子圖模型所提供的三個不同特性，並推導出三個研究問題，每個特性一個，探討如何在時間序列中利用每個特性：RQ1。圖的拓撲和潛能是直接可編程的原始元件。這是否可以用來通過結構圖修改將符號時間序列先驗注入 ST-PT，特別是在數據稀缺和噪聲的情況下？RQ2。CRF 的因子矩陣是運算子的潛能。外部條件能否在每個樣本的基礎上編程這些因子矩陣，使得條件生成成為結構性而非固定一個的特徵級調制？RQ3。每次 MFVI 迭代都是因子圖上的貝葉斯後驗更新。這是否能將潛在空間自回歸（AR）預測的潛在轉換從不透明的 MLP 轉變為有原則的後驗更新，並且 CRF 教師能否將其潛在轉化為 AR 學生以抵消累積誤差？我們針對每個問題提供一項實證研究。這三項研究共同將 ST-PT 定位為一個可編程的時間序列建模框架。

##### **FutureWorld: A Live Environment for Training Predictive Agents with Real-World Outcome Rewards**
2604.26733v1 by Zhixin Han, Yanzhi Zhang, Chuyang Wei, Maohang Gao, Xiawei Yue, Kefei Chen, Yu Zhuang, Haoxiang Guan, Jiyan He, Jian Li, Yitong Duan, Yu Shi, Mengting Hu, Shuxin Zheng

Live future prediction refers to the task of making predictions about real-world events before they unfold. This task is increasingly studied using large language model-based agent systems, and it is important for building agents that can continually learn from real-world. Just as interactive environments have often driven progress in agents, advancing live future prediction naturally motivates viewing it as a learning environment. Prior works have explored future prediction from several different parts, but have generally not framed it as a unified learning environment. This task is appealing for learning because it can provide a large number of prediction questions grounded in diverse real-world events, while preventing answer leakage. To leverage the advantages of live future prediction, we present FutureWorld, a live agentic reinforcement learning environment that closes the training loop between prediction, outcome realization, and parameters update. In our environment, we take three open-source base models and train them for consecutive days. The results show that training is effective. Furthermore, we build a daily benchmark based on the environment and evaluate several frontier agents on it to establish performance baselines for current agent systems.

摘要：即時未來預測是指在現實事件展開之前對其進行預測的任務。<lb/>這項任務越來越多地使用基於大型語言模型的代理系統進行研究，對於構建能夠不斷從現實世界學習的代理來說，這是非常重要的。<lb/>正如互動環境經常推動代理的進步一樣，推進即時未來預測自然促使將其視為一個學習環境。<lb/>先前的研究從幾個不同的方面探討了未來預測，但通常沒有將其框架化為一個統一的學習環境。<lb/>這項任務對於學習來說是有吸引力的，因為它可以提供大量基於多樣化現實事件的預測問題，同時防止答案洩漏。<lb/>為了利用即時未來預測的優勢，我們提出了FutureWorld，一個即時代理強化學習環境，該環境關閉了預測、結果實現和參數更新之間的訓練循環。<lb/>在我們的環境中，我們選取三個開源基礎模型並對其進行連續幾天的訓練。<lb/>結果顯示訓練是有效的。<lb/>此外，我們基於該環境建立了一個每日基準，並在其上評估幾個前沿代理，以建立當前代理系統的性能基準。

##### **Swap distance minimization shapes the order of subject, object and verb in languages of the world**
2604.26726v1 by Jairo Rios-El-Yazidi, Ramon Ferrer-i-Cancho

Languages of the world vary concerning the order of subject, object and verb. The most frequent dominant orders are SOV and SVO, and researchers have tailored models to this fact. However, there are still languages whose dominant order does not conform to these expectations or even lack a dominant order. Here we show that across linguistic families and macroareas, word order variation within languages is shaped by the principle of swap distance minimization even when the dominant order is not SOV/SVO and even when a dominant order is lacking.

摘要：世界的語言在主語、賓語和動詞的順序上有所不同。最常見的主要順序是SOV和SVO，研究人員已根據這一事實調整了模型。然後，仍然存在一些語言，其主要順序不符合這些預期，甚至缺乏主要順序。在這裡，我們展示了在語言家族和宏觀區域之間，語言內部的詞序變異是由交換距離最小化原則所塑造，即使主要順序不是SOV/SVO，甚至在缺乏主要順序的情況下也是如此。

##### **A self-evolving agent for explainable diagnosis of DFT-experiment band-gap mismatch**
2604.26703v1 by Yue Li, Bijun Tang

Standard density functional theory (DFT) routinely misclassifies the electronic ground state of correlated and structurally complex compounds, predicting metallic behaviour for materials that experiments report as semiconductors. Each such mismatch encodes a specific non-ideality -- magnetic ordering, electron correlation, an alternative polymorph, or a defect -- that the calculation excluded, but extracting that signal at scale has remained a manual exercise. Here we introduce XDFT, a closed-loop agent that diagnoses the mismatch automatically: it draws candidate hypotheses from a curated catalogue, executes the corresponding first-principles tests, and updates a global Bayesian posterior over hypothesis usefulness from each verdict. On a verified benchmark of 124 materials, XDFT identifies a resolving mechanism for 70 of 90 mismatch cases (78\%), an order of magnitude above a uniform-random baseline (19\%) and a static LLM ordering (20\%). The internal posterior aligns with empirical performance over the benchmark timeline, and resolved cases collapse into a tri-partite element-class taxonomy that we distil into a four-line static rule. Each diagnosed material is returned with a corrected protocol and a mechanistic attribution; failed cases are flagged as evidence-backed targets for experimental re-examination.

摘要：標準密度泛函理論 (DFT) 通常錯誤地將相關和結構複雜的化合物的電子基態分類，預測金屬行為的材料卻被實驗報告為半導體。每一個這樣的錯配都編碼了一個特定的非理想性——磁序、電子相關、替代多型或缺陷——這些計算未能考慮，但在大規模提取該信號仍然是一項手動工作。在此，我們介紹 XDFT，一個自動診斷錯配的閉環代理：它從經過策劃的目錄中提取候選假設，執行相應的第一性原理測試，並根據每個判決更新假設有效性的全球貝葉斯後驗。在一個經過驗證的 124 種材料基準上，XDFT 為 90 個錯配案例中的 70 個（78%）識別出了解決機制，這比均勻隨機基線（19%）和靜態 LLM 排序（20%）高出一個數量級。內部後驗與基準時間線上的實證表現一致，解決的案例歸納為一個三部分元素類別分類法，我們將其提煉為一條四行靜態規則。每個診斷的材料都會返回一個修正的協議和機制歸因；失敗的案例則被標記為有證據支持的實驗重新檢查目標。

##### **Unified 4D World Action Modeling from Video Priors with Asynchronous Denoising**
2604.26694v1 by Jun Guo, Qiwei Li, Peiyan Li, Zilong Chen, Nan Sun, Yifei Su, Heyun Wang, Yuan Zhang, Xinghang Li, Huaping Liu

We propose X-WAM, a Unified 4D World Model that unifies real-time robotic action execution and high-fidelity 4D world synthesis (video + 3D reconstruction) in a single framework, addressing the critical limitations of prior unified world models (e.g., UWM) that only model 2D pixel-space and fail to balance action efficiency and world modeling quality. To leverage the strong visual priors of pretrained video diffusion models, X-WAM imagines the future world by predicting multi-view RGB-D videos, and obtains spatial information efficiently through a lightweight structural adaptation: replicating the final few blocks of the pretrained Diffusion Transformer into a dedicated depth prediction branch for the reconstruction of future spatial information. Moreover, we propose Asynchronous Noise Sampling (ANS) to jointly optimize generation quality and action decoding efficiency. ANS applies a specialized asynchronous denoising schedule during inference, which rapidly decodes actions with fewer steps to enable efficient real-time execution, while dedicating the full sequence of steps to generate high-fidelity video. Rather than entirely decoupling the timesteps during training, ANS samples from their joint distribution to align with the inference distribution. Pretrained on over 5,800 hours of robotic data, X-WAM achieves 79.2% and 90.7% average success rate on RoboCasa and RoboTwin 2.0 benchmarks, while producing high-fidelity 4D reconstruction and generation surpassing existing methods in both visual and geometric metrics.

摘要：我們提出了 X-WAM，一個統一的 4D 世界模型，將實時機器人行動執行和高保真 4D 世界合成（視頻 + 3D 重建）統一在一個框架中，解決了先前統一世界模型（例如 UWM）的關鍵限制，這些模型僅建模 2D 像素空間，並未能平衡行動效率和世界建模質量。為了利用預訓練視頻擴散模型的強大視覺先驗，X-WAM 通過預測多視角 RGB-D 視頻來想像未來世界，並通過輕量級結構適應有效獲取空間信息：將預訓練擴散Transformer的最後幾個區塊複製到專用的深度預測分支，以重建未來的空間信息。此外，我們提出了異步噪聲採樣（ANS），以共同優化生成質量和行動解碼效率。ANS 在推理過程中應用專門的異步去噪時間表，快速以較少的步驟解碼行動，以實現高效的實時執行，同時將完整的步驟序列專注於生成高保真的視頻。在訓練期間，ANS 並未完全解耦時間步，而是從它們的聯合分佈中進行採樣，以與推理分佈對齊。X-WAM 在超過 5800 小時的機器人數據上進行預訓練，在 RoboCasa 和 RoboTwin 2.0 基準上達到了 79.2% 和 90.7% 的平均成功率，同時生成的高保真 4D 重建和生成在視覺和幾何指標上超越了現有方法。

##### **From Black-Box Confidence to Measurable Trust in Clinical AI: A Framework for Evidence, Supervision, and Staged Autonomy**
2604.26671v1 by Serhii Zabolotnii, Viktoriia Holinko, Olha Antonenko

Trust in clinical artificial intelligence (AI) cannot be reduced to model accuracy, fluency of generation, or overall positive user impression. In medicine, trust must be engineered as a measurable system property grounded in evidence, supervision, and operational boundaries of AI autonomy. This article proposes a practical framework for trustworthy clinical AI built around three principles: evidence, supervision, and staged autonomy. Rather than replacing deterministic clinical logic wholesale with end-to-end black-box models, the proposed approach combines a deterministic core, a patient-specific AI assistant for contextual validation, a multi-tier model escalation mechanism, and a human supervision layer for verification, escalation, and risk control. We demonstrate that trust also depends on selective verification of clinically critical findings, bounded clinical context, disciplined prompt architecture, and careful evaluation on realistic cases. Classifier-driven modular prompting is examined as an incremental path to scaling clinical depth without sacrificing prompt performance and without waiting for complete rule-based coverage. To operationalize trust, a set of trust metrics is proposed, built on metrological principles -- measurement uncertainty, calibration, traceability -- enabling quantitative rather than subjective assessment of each architectural layer. In this perspective, trustworthy clinical AI emerges not as a property of an individual model, but as an architectural outcome of a system into which evidence trails, human oversight, tiered escalation, and graduated action rights are embedded from the outset.

##### **Differentially-Private Text Rewriting reshapes Linguistic Style**
2604.26656v1 by Stefan Arnold

Differential Privacy (DP) for text matured from disjointed word-level substitutions to contiguous sentence-level rewriting by leveraging the generative capacity of language models. While this form of text privatization is best suited for balancing formal privacy guarantees with grammatical coherence, its impact on the register identity of text remains largely unexplored. By conducting a multidimensional stylistic profiling of differentially-private rewriting, we demonstrate that the cost of privacy extends far beyond lexical variation. Specifically, we find that rewriting under privacy constraints induces a systematic functional mutation of the text's communicative signature. This shift is characterized by the severe attrition of interactive markers, contextual references, and complex subordination. By comparing autoregressive paraphrasing against bidirectional substitution across a spectrum of privacy budgets, we observe that both architectures force convergence toward a non-involved and non-persuasive register. This register-blind sanitization effectively preserves semantic content but structurally homogenizes the nuanced stylistic markers that define human-authored discourse.

摘要：差分隱私（DP）對於文本的發展從不連貫的單詞級替換轉向連續的句子級重寫，利用了語言模型的生成能力。雖然這種文本私密化形式最適合平衡正式的隱私保證與語法連貫性，但其對文本註冊身份的影響仍然大多未被探索。通過對差分私密重寫進行多維度的風格分析，我們證明隱私的成本遠超過詞彙變化。具體來說，我們發現，在隱私限制下的重寫會導致文本傳達特徵的系統性功能突變。這一變化的特徵是互動標記、上下文參考和複雜從屬關係的嚴重減少。通過比較自回歸性改寫與雙向替換在不同隱私預算範圍內的表現，我們觀察到這兩種架構都迫使文本向一種非參與性和非說服性的註冊趨近。這種對註冊盲目的清理有效地保留了語義內容，但在結構上同質化了定義人類創作話語的細微風格標記。

##### **When to Retrieve During Reasoning: Adaptive Retrieval for Large Reasoning Models**
2604.26649v1 by Dongxin Guo, Jikun Wu, Siu Ming Yiu

Large reasoning models such as DeepSeek-R1 and OpenAI o1 generate extended chains of thought spanning thousands of tokens, yet their integration with retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) remains fundamentally misaligned. Current RAG systems optimize for providing context before reasoning begins, while reasoning models require evidence injection during multi-step inference chains. We introduce ReaLM-Retrieve, a reasoning-aware retrieval framework that addresses this mismatch through three key innovations: (1) a step-level uncertainty detector that identifies knowledge gaps at reasoning-step granularity rather than token or sentence level; (2) a retrieval intervention policy that learns when external evidence maximally benefits ongoing reasoning; and (3) an efficiency-optimized integration mechanism that reduces per-retrieval overhead by 3.2x compared to naive integration. Experiments on MuSiQue, HotpotQA, and 2WikiMultiHopQA demonstrate that ReaLM-Retrieve achieves on average 10.1% absolute improvement in answer F1 over standard RAG (range: 9.0-11.8% across the three benchmarks) while reducing retrieval calls by 47% compared to fixed-interval approaches like IRCoT (all improvements significant at p<0.01, paired bootstrap). On the challenging MuSiQue benchmark requiring 2-4 hop reasoning, our method achieves 71.2% F1 with an average of only 1.8 retrieval calls per question. Analysis shows that ReaLM-Retrieve also improves retrieval quality itself, achieving 81.3% Recall@5 with consistently higher precision and MRR than fixed-interval baselines on supporting evidence, establishing new state-of-the-art efficiency-accuracy trade-offs for reasoning-intensive retrieval tasks.

摘要：大型推理模型如 DeepSeek-R1 和 OpenAI o1 生成延伸的思考鏈，跨越數千個標記，但它們與檢索增強生成（RAG）的整合仍然根本不對齊。當前的 RAG 系統優化於在推理開始之前提供上下文，而推理模型則需要在多步推理鏈中進行證據注入。我們介紹了 ReaLM-Retrieve，一個考慮推理的檢索框架，通過三個關鍵創新來解決這一不匹配問題：（1）一個步驟級的不確定性檢測器，能夠在推理步驟的粒度上識別知識缺口，而不是在標記或句子級別；（2）一個檢索干預政策，學習何時外部證據對正在進行的推理帶來最大益處；（3）一個效率優化的整合機制，與天真的整合相比，每次檢索的開銷減少了 3.2 倍。對 MuSiQue、HotpotQA 和 2WikiMultiHopQA 的實驗顯示，ReaLM-Retrieve 在答案 F1 上平均實現了 10.1% 的絕對提升，相對於標準 RAG（在三個基準上範圍：9.0-11.8%），同時與固定間隔方法如 IRCoT 相比，檢索調用減少了 47%（所有改進在 p&lt;0.01 的配對自助法下顯著）。在需要 2-4 步推理的挑戰性 MuSiQue 基準上，我們的方法實現了 71.2% 的 F1，每個問題平均僅需 1.8 次檢索調用。分析顯示，ReaLM-Retrieve 還改善了檢索質量，實現了 81.3% 的 Recall@5，並在支持證據上始終保持比固定間隔基準更高的精確度和 MRR，為推理密集型檢索任務建立了新的最先進效率-準確性權衡。

##### **SciHorizon-DataEVA: An Agentic System for AI-Readiness Evaluation of Heterogeneous Scientific Data**
2604.26645v1 by Dianyu Liu, Chuan Qin, Xi Chen, Xiaohan Li, Wenxi Xu, Yuyang Wang, Xin Chen, Yuanchun Zhou, Hengshu Zhu

In this work, we propose SciHorizon-DataEVA, a novel agentic system to scalable AI-readiness evaluation of heterogeneous scientific data. At the evaluation-criteria level, we introduce the Sci-TQA2 principles, which organize AI-readiness into four complementary dimensions: Governance Trustworthiness, Data Quality, AI Compatibility, and Scientific Adaptability. Each dimension is decomposed into measurable atomic elements that enable fine-grained and executable assessment. To operationalize these principles at scale, we develop Sci-TQA2-Eval, a hierarchical multi-agent evaluation approach orchestrated through a directed, cyclic workflow. Our Sci-TQA2-Eval dynamically constructs dataset-aware evaluation specifications by combining lightweight dataset profiling, applicability-aware metric activation, and knowledge-augmented planning grounded in domain constraints and dataset-paper signals. These specifications are executed through an adaptive, tool-centric evaluation mechanism with built-in verification and self-correction, enabling scalable and reliable assessment across heterogeneous scientific data.
